***угощать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:угощать.html>угоща́ть</a> (6137)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Fom <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угостить.html>угости́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ugostítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гостить.html>гости́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gostítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be on visit, to stay</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See there for more
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угощать.html>угоща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ugoščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угостить.html>угости́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to treat <i>(someone, to something)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:угощать.html>угоща́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:обед.html>обе́дом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ugoščátʹ</b> kovó-libo obédom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to treat someone to lunch</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to entertain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посмотреть.html>посмотрите</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сынок.html>сынка́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:угощаемый.html>угоща́ем</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">posmotrite kak synká <b>ugoščájem</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">See how we <b>entertain</b> the kids</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***угощение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:угощение.html>угоще́ние</a> (10740)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угощать.html>угоща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ugoščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угощение.html>угоще́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ugoščénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угощение.html>угоще́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угощение.html>угоще́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угощение.html>угоще́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>treat, food, fare, entertainment (with something)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:угробить.html>угро́бить</a> (17085)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угробить.html>угро́бить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ugróbitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гробить.html>гро́бить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to kill, to do to death, to give the business</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to throw away, to burn up, to send down the drain</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:угрожать.html>угрожа́ть</a> (4257)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Verbal form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угроза.html>угро́за</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ugróza</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">threat, danger</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гроза.html>гроза́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grozá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">terror</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*groza</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">terror</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (vd. there for cognates)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угрожать.html>угрожа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ugrožátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>

***угрюмо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:угрюмый.html>угрю́мо</a> (5619)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угрюмый.html>угрю́мый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ugrjúmyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угрюмый.html>угрю́мо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ugrjúmo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>morosely, sullenly</li>
<li>bleakly, forbiddingly</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угрюмый.html>угрю́мый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ugrjúmyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***удав.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удав.html>уда́в</a> (3772)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Verbal noun of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удавить.html>удави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udavítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удав.html>уда́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udáv</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удав.html>уда́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удав.html>уда́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удав.html>уда́вов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>boa constrictor</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***удавиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удавиться.html>удави́ться</a> (20687)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удавить.html>удави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udavítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удавиться.html>удави́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udavítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">уда́вливаться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to strangle oneself, to hang oneself</li>

***удавка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удавка.html>уда́вка</a> (24605)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удавить.html>удави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udavítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удавка.html>уда́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udávka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удавка.html>уда́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удавка.html>уда́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удавка.html>уда́вок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>running knot, slip-knot, timber-hitch</li>
<li>garrote, any kind of choking weapon</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">уда́вливать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">udávlivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удавить.html>удави́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">udavítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***удаление.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удаление.html>удале́ние</a> (7380)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удалить.html>удали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удаление.html>удале́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udalénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удаление.html>удале́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удаление.html>удале́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удаление.html>удале́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>moving off, moving away</li>
<li>sending away
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удаление.html>удале́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поле.html>по́ля</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udalénije</b> s pólja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sending off the field</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>deletion, removal <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">the act of deleting</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удаление.html>удале́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:файл.html>фа́йла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udalénije</b> fájla</i> ― <span class="e-translation">deletion of a file</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>ablation, surgical removal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удаление.html>удале́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зу́ба</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udalénije</b> zúba</i> ― <span class="e-translation">extraction of a tooth</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удаление.html>удале́ние</a></b> адено́идов</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udalénije</b> adɛnóidov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">adenoidectomy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удаление.html>удале́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:желчный.html>же́лчного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пузырь.html>пузыря́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udalénije</b> žélčnovo puzyrjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cholecystectomy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удаление.html>удале́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:матка.html>ма́тки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udalénije</b> mátki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hysterectomy</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:даль.html>даль</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dalʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***удалить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удалить.html>удали́ть</a> (11588)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-дали́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-dalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удалить.html>удали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udalítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удалять.html>удаля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to remove
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удалить.html>удали́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зуб</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udalítʹ</b> zub</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to extract a tooth</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to send away, to dismiss
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удалить.html>удали́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:игрок.html>игрока́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поле.html>по́ля</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udalítʹ</b> igroká s pólja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to send a player off the field</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to delete
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удалить.html>удали́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:файл.html>файл</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udalítʹ</b> fajl</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to delete a file</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put off, to postpone</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">postpone</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдалить.html>отдали́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otdalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***удалять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удалять.html>удаля́ть</a> (13767)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удалить.html>удали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удалять.html>удаля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udaljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удалить.html>удали́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to remove
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удалять.html>удаля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зуб</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udaljátʹ</b> zub</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to extract a tooth</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to send away, to dismiss
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удалять.html>удаля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:игрок.html>игрока́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поле.html>по́ля</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udaljátʹ</b> igroká s pólja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to send a player off the field</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to delete
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удалять.html>удаля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:файл.html>файл</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udaljátʹ</b> fajl</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to delete a file</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put off, to postpone</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">postpone</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отдаля́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otdaljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удар.html>удар</a> (614)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удар.html>уда́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udár</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удар.html>уда́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удар.html>уда́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удар.html>уда́ров</a></b>)

<ol><li>hit, blow, strike</li>
